				Brothel gets tick to triple staff

Caryn Metcalfe

AN ARTARMON brothel has tripled the number of sex workers on site with approval from Willoughby Council.

Miss Heavens, at 6 Cleg St, Artarmon, was taken over by Comm Database in August 2016 and began renovations to suit demand.

The operator applied to the council in February to modify its approval conditions to increase the number of work rooms from seven to nine. They also asked to increase the number of sex workers on site from five to 15 and the hours of operation from 11am-3am seven days to 24 hour a day, seven days a week.

Council officers assessing the application noted that as street parking demand was low during the off-peak, or night-time, period, an increase in staff numbers from 5pm to 7am could be supported.

However, it recommended the day period remain at five and the company people mover be provided to transport staff to and from the site.

The council approved the application, with five sex workers and three administration staff daytime, Monday to Friday, and 15 sex workers and three administration staff at night-time on weekdays and 24 hours on weekends and public holidays.
